GlobalKTable}, or can be aggregated into a {@link KTable}.\n * A {@link KStream} can also be directly {@link KStream#toTable() converted} into a {@code KTable}.\n * Kafka Streams DSL can be understanding how DSL operations like map, filter, and groupBy are implemented using the lower-level Processor API.\\n\\nCore Processor API Components:\\n1. Processor (processor/api/Processor.java) - Base interface for implementing stateless record processing\\n2. ProcessorSupplier (processor/api/ProcessorSupplier.java) - Factory for creating Processor instances\\n3. FixedKeyProcessor (processor/api/FixedKeyProcessor.java) - Processor variant for operations with fixed/unchanged keys\\n4. FixedKeyProcessorSupplier (processor/api/FixedKeyProcessorSupplier.java) - Factory for FixedKeyProcessor instances\\n5. Record (processor/api/Record.java) - Represents individual records with key, value, metadata\\n6. ContextualProcessor & ContextualFixedKeyProcessor - Base classes that provide context access\\n\\nDSL Operation Implementations:\\nEach DSL operation is implemented as a ProcessorSupplier that creates Processor instances:\\n\\n1. Filter Operations:\\n   - KStreamFilter (kstream/internals/KStreamFilter.java) - Implements FixedKeyProcessorSupplier, uses ContextualFixedKeyProcessor\\n   - KTableFilter (kstream/internals/KTableFilter.java) - For table-based filtering\\n   - Uses Predicate interface for filtering logic\\n\\n2. Map Operations:\\n   - KStreamMap (kstream/internals/KStreamMap.java) - Implements ProcessorSupplier for key-value mapping\\n   - KStreamMapValues (kstream/internals/KStreamMapValues.java) - Maps only values, preserves keys (FixedKeyProcessorSupplier)\\n   - KTableMapValues (kstream/internals/KTableMapValues.java) - Table variant\\n   - Uses KeyValueMapper for transformation\\n\\n3. FlatMap Operations:\\n   - KStreamFlatMap (kstream/internals/KStreamFlatMap.java) - Implements ProcessorSupplier for flattening key-value pairs\\n   - KStreamFlatMapValues (kstream/internals/KStreamFlatMapValues.java) - Flattens values only\\n   - Returns Iterable<KeyValue<K, V>> for multiple output records per input\\n\\n4. Aggregation Operations:\\n   - KStreamAggregate (kstream/internals/KStreamAggregate.java) - ProcessorSupplier for stream aggregation\\n   - KStreamReduce (kstream/internals/KStreamReduce.java) - Reducer implementation\\n   - KStreamWindowAggregate - Windowed aggregation variant\\n   - KTableAggregate, KTableReduce - Table aggregation variants\\n   - Use Initializer, Aggregator, and Reducer interfaces\\n\\n5. GroupBy Operations:\\n   - KGroupedStreamImpl (kstream/internals/KGroupedStreamImpl.java) - Represents grouped streams\\n   - KGroupedTableImpl (kstream/internals/KGroupedTableImpl.java) - Represents grouped tables\\n   - Requires repartitioning with KStreamRepartitionMap\\n\\nDSL Interface Classes:\\n- KStream (kstream/KStream.java) - Main DSL interface defining filter, map, flatMap, groupBy operations\\n- KTable (kstream/KTable.java) - Table DSL interface\\n- KGroupedStream (kstream/KGroupedStream.java) - Grouped stream interface\\n- KGroupedTable (kstream/KGroupedTable.java) - Grouped table interface\\n\\nImplementation Classes:\\n- KStreamImpl (kstream/internals/KStreamImpl.java) - Implements KStream interface, creates ProcessorSupplier instances\\n- KTableImpl (kstream/internals/KTableImpl.java) - Implements KTable interface\\n- These classes use InternalStreamsBuilder to add processor nodes to topology\\n\\nKey Pattern:\\nDSL methods create ProcessorGraphNode instances with ProcessorParameters containing the appropriate ProcessorSupplier (e.g., new KStreamFilter(), new KStreamMap()). The topology builder integrates these into the execution graph. The ProcessorSupplier.get() method returns a Processor instance that extends ContextualProcessor or ContextualFixedKeyProcessor, implementing the actual processing logic via the process() method.\\n\\nFor custom state store management during migration, users can:\\n1. Replace DSL operations with Processor API using ProcessorSupplier\\n2. Implement custom Processor classes extending ContextualProcessor/ContextualFixedKeyProcessor\\n3. Access ProcessorContext for state store management\\n4. Use Topology.addProcessor() or StreamsBuilder.addStateStore() for state store configuration\\n\\nRelated Resources:\\n- StreamsBuilder (StreamsBuilder.java) - Utility for building topologies with DSL\\n- Topology (Topology.java) - Lower-level topology definition using Processor API\\n- ProcessorContext implementations handle record forwarding and state store access\"\n}\nEOF\ncat /workspace/answer.json\n","description":"Create comprehensive answer.json with findings"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2879,"cache_read_input_tokens":51178,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":2879},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"a19e7345-566f-42c6-831a-728845dcda87","uuid":"51d46361-1282-49b9-b6ff-f69ae56079b0"}

FixedKeyProcessorSupplier (processor/api/FixedKeyProcessorSupplier.java) - Factory for FixedKeyProcessor instances\\n5. Map Operations:\\n   - KStreamMap (kstream/internals/KStreamMap.java) - Implements ProcessorSupplier for key-value mapping\\n   - KStreamMapValues (kstream/internals/KStreamMapValues.java) - Maps only values, preserves keys (FixedKeyProcessorSupplier)\\n   - KTableMapValues (kstream/internals/KTableMapValues.java) - Table variant\\n   - Uses KeyValueMapper for transformation\\n\\n3.
